**Findings**

- **P1** — [§6.3.1 lines 762-772](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:762>), [§6.1 lines 611-635](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:611>), [§14.1 line 1708](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:1708>)  
  **Description:** Phase 2 still depends on the Phase 3 classifier surface because `createBrief` types `uiContext` as `ChatTriageInput['uiContext']`, but `ChatTriageInput` is only specified under the Phase 3 fast-path classifier rather than the Phase 2 shared type package.  
  **Recommendation:** Move the request-facing UI context type into a Phase 2 shared types file (`shared/types/briefFastPath.ts` or a sibling), and have `createBrief`/`POST /api/briefs` depend on that shared type instead of a classifier-owned type.

- **P1** — [§5.3 lines 487-507](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:487>), [§5.3 lines 534-536](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:534>), [§11 Phase 5 line 1500](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:1500>), [§14.2 line 1821](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:1821>)  
  **Description:** The `0ZZZ` migration prose says `memory_blocks` gains a `quality_score` mirror column, but the actual SQL block for that migration never adds `quality_score`.  
  **Recommendation:** Add the `quality_score` column definition to the `0ZZZ_memory_blocks_precedence_and_deprecation.sql` spec block and keep the migration, schema-file inventory, and Phase 5 scope text aligned.

- **P1** — [§3.1 line 134](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:134>), [§8.7 lines 1278-1280](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:1278>), [§11 Phase 2 lines 1439-1451](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:1439>), [§7 lines 1097-1152](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:1097>)  
  **Description:** The spec says Task chat ships in Phase 2 and Agent-run-log chat ships in Phase 7, but §7 only defines Brief routes/streaming and never defines the route or socket contract that those non-Brief conversation panes would use.  
  **Recommendation:** Either add explicit task/agent-run conversation endpoints and room semantics to §7/§10/§11, or descope those panes until a generic conversation route surface is specified.

- **P2** — [§6.1 line 653](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:653>), [§10 line 1378](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:1378>), [§14.1-14.2 lines 1721-1829](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:1721>)  
  **Description:** Shadow-eval outcome recording is described as a direct `fastPathDecisionLogger.recordOutcome(...)` call in §6.1 but as an async fire-and-forget queued task in §10, and the async path has no named file/job in the inventory.  
  **Recommendation:** Pick one execution model, then name and inventory the concrete mechanism (`fastPathDecisionLogger` sync call or a dedicated outcome-recorder job/service) and specify its idempotency/update semantics.

- **P2** — [§11 Phase 0 exit gate line 1410](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:1410>), [§12.2 line 1641](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:1641>), [§3.2 line 140](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:140>), [§14.3 line 1845](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:1845>)  
  **Description:** Phase 0 is internally inconsistent about the harness example and quietly pulls an out-of-scope branch into the critical path: the exit gate says “synthetic capability,” while §12.2 says the example capability is the CRM Query Planner contract test from a separate branch.  
  **Recommendation:** Keep Phase 0 self-contained by requiring only a local synthetic/example fixture in this spec, and move CRM Planner harness adoption to optional cross-branch coordination under Phase 9.

- **P2** — [§4.6 lines 334-341](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:334>), [§5.3 lines 521-524](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:521>), [§6.3.2 lines 793-799](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:793>), [§9.5 lines 1333-1338](</C:/Files/Projects/automation-v1-2nd/docs/universal-brief-dev-spec.md:1333>)  
  **Description:** `isAuthoritative` is load-bearing because authoritative rules outrank scope, but the spec does not pin any stricter governance mechanism than ordinary `rules.write`, so “authoritative” is effectively just a client-supplied boolean.  
  **Recommendation:** Define who may set/clear `is_authoritative` with a named permission or role check in `ruleCaptureService`/`PATCH /api/rules/:ruleId`, or remove the authoritative tier from v1 until that governance exists.
